<script type="text/javascript">
$(window).on("message", function(e) {
    var data = e.originalEvent.data;
	$('.block_flash_video_iframe').height(data.height);
	$('.block_flash_video').height(data.height);

});

$(document).ready(function(){
	var owl = $(".list_video #owl-demo");
	owl.owlCarousel({
		autoPlay: 7000,
		items : 3,
		itemsDesktop : [1199,3],
		itemsTablet: [600,2], //2 items between 600 and 0
		itemsDesktopSmall : [900,3],// betweem 900px and 601px
		itemsMobile		:[479,2],
		pagination:false,
        	});
    	$(".list_video .next_slider").click(function(){
		owl.trigger('owl.next');
	});
	$(".list_video .prev_slider").click(function(){
		owl.trigger('owl.prev');
	});
    });
